zn-body zn--idx-0 zn-has-multiple-containers zn-has-13-containers" data-containers="13" data-eq-pts="xsmall: 0, medium: 460, large: 780, full16x9: 1100" data-vr-zone="zone-1-0" data-zn-id="body-text" data-zone-label="bodyText" id="body-text"><div class="l-container"><div class="el__leafmedia el__leafmedia--storyhighlights"><div class="el__storyhighlights_wrapper"><div class="el__storyhighlights"><h3 class="el__headline">Story highlights</h3><ul class="el__storyhighlights__list"><li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">The billionaire GOP presidential candidate joins global peace negotiators and war survivors</li><li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">Edward Snowden hasn also been nominated for the award</li><li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">President Barack Obama won the award in 2009</li></ul></div><div class="ad ad--epic" data-ad-text="show"><div class="ad-ad_ns_btf_01 ad-refresh-default" id="ad_ns_btf_01"></div></div></div></div><div class="el__leafmedia el__leafmedia--sourced-paragraph"><p class="zn-body__paragraph"><cite class="el-editorial-source"> (CNN)</cite><a href="http://www.cnn.com/2015/10/09/world/nobel-peace-prize-5-things-to-know/index.html">Nobel Peace Prize</a> nominees: The Greek island groups welcoming Syrian refugees, an escaped ISIS sex slave turned women\'s rights activist, the negotiators who ended five decades of civil war in Colombia, National Security Agency leaker Edward Snowden.</p></div><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Oh, and <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2013/07/04/us/donald-trump-fast-facts/">Donald Trump</a>.</p><div class="ad ad--epic ad--mobile" data-ad-text="show"><div class="ad-ad_rect_btf_02 ad-refresh-default" id="ad_rect_btf_02"></div></div><ul class="cn cn-list-hierarchical-xs cn--idx-4 cn-zoneAdContainer"></ul><p class="zn-body__paragraph">The Republican presidential candidate, who was hosting a reality TV show at this time last year, has been nominated for the 2016 Nobel Peace Prize by a mystery patron, Kristian Berg Harpviken told CNN on Wednesday, confirming an earlier <a href="http://news.yahoo.com/trump-greek-islanders-running-nobel-prize-233705715.html" target="_blank">AFP report</a>.</p><div class="el__embedded CNN.AdSlide(\'el__gallery\', false, CNN.contentModel.singletonFile);});</script></div></div></div><p class="zn-body__paragraph">A respected Nobel watcher and director of the Peace Research Institute of Oslo, Harpviken said he was "committed to not reveal the nominator\'s name," but shared online <a href="https://www.prio.org/About/PeacePrize/PRIO-Directors-Speculations-2016/" target="_blank">the language</a> from the letter, which praised Trump for "his vigorous peace through strength ideology, used as a threat weapon of deterrence against radical Islam, ISIS, nuclear Iran and Communist China."</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">During his campaign, Trump has repeatedly vowed to "bomb the s-- out of ISIS" and threatened to impose a protective tariff on trade with the Chinese.</p><div class="zn-body__read-more"><div class="read-more-gradient"></div><div class="read-more-button"><div class="read-more-link" id="js-body-read-more">Read More</div></div></div><div class="zn-body__read-all"><p class="zn-body__paragraph">The Nobel Committee, which does not reveal the details of its decision-making process, typically offers thousands of people the opportunity to nominate notable organizations and individuals for the award, which counts among its recipients Martin Luther King Jr., the Red Cross and, in <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/europe/10/09/nobel.peace.prize/index.html">2009, President Barack Obama</a>.</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Trump, however, is not on Harpviken\'s shortlist, which is currently topped by Snowden and two top U.S. and Iranian nuclear negotiators. Others who were nominated but did not receive the prize include Mahatma Gandhi, Pope Francis, Adolf Hitler and Vladimir Putin. </p></div><p class="zn-body__paragraph zn-body__footer">CORRECTION: An earlier version of this story incorrectly stated Henry Kissinger did not receive the Nobel Peace Prize; he was given the award in 1973.</p></div><div class="zn-body__read-more-outbrain"><ul class="cn
